#     PROJECT                  STP>Solar Terrestrial Probes
#     SOURCE_NAME              stb>Solar Terrestrial Relations Observatory Behind the Sun-Earth Line
#     DISCIPLINE               Solar Physics>Heliospheric Physics
#     DATA_TYPE                COHO1HR>1 Hour Time Resolution from cohoweb
#     DESCRIPTOR               MAG_PLASMA>Merged Trajectory, Magnetic Field, and Plasma
#     DATA_VERSION             1
#     TEXT                     The Solar-Terrestrial Relations Observatory (STEREO) mission includes two spacecraft                   
#     TEXT                      respectively lagging (STEREO A) and leading (STEREO B) the Earth in heliocentric                      
#     TEXT                      orbit around the Sun for remote 3-D imaging and radio observations of coronal                         
#     TEXT                      mass ejections (CMEs).  These events are responsible for large solar energetic                        
#     TEXT                      particle events in interplanetary space and are the primary cause of major                            
#     TEXT                      geomagnetic storms at Earth. The two spacecraft are launched to drift slowly                          
#     TEXT                      away from the Earth in opposite directions at about 10 degrees per year for                           
#     TEXT                      the lagging spacecraft and 20 degrees per year for the leading one. Optimal                           
#     TEXT                      longitudinal separation of about sixty degrees is achieved after two years.                           
#     TEXT                      Afterwards the separation gradually increases beyond the design lifetime of                           
#     TEXT                      two years with the possibility of extended mission observations at larger angles.                     
#     TEXT                      Science instruments selected for STEREO include the Sun Earth Connection Coronal                      
#     TEXT                      and Heliospheric Investigation (SECCHI) for extreme ultraviolet (EUV), white-light                    
#     TEXT                      coronographic, and heliospheric imaging, the STEREO/WAVES (SWAVES) interplanetary                     
#     TEXT                      radio burst tracker, the In situ Measurements of Particles and CME Transients                         
#     TEXT                      (IMPACT) investigation for in-situ sampling the 3-D distribution and plasma                           
#     TEXT                      characteristics of solar energetic particles and the interplanetary magnetic                          
#     TEXT                      field, and the PLAsma and SupraThermal Ion and Composition (PLASTIC) experiment                       
#     TEXT                      to measure elemental and charge composition of ambient and CME plasma ions.                           
#     TEXT                      STEREO data recorded and stored onboard each spacecraft will be downlinked                            
#     TEXT                      through the NASA Deep Space Network on a daily schedule. Real-time space weather                      
#     TEXT                      data will be continuously transmitted through a separate beacon system to NASA                        
#                               and non-NASA receiving stations.                                                                      
#                              About STEREO data in COHOWEB STEREO-A and -B data are from the magnetometer                            
#                               of the IMPACT package and from the PLASTIC plasma detector.  Principal Investigators                  
#                               for these packages are Janet Luhmann (UCB) and Antoinette Galvin (UNH), respectively.                 
#                                Magnetic field  data were obtained as 10-min averages from the UCLA web site                         
#                               at http://aten.igpp.ucla.edu/forms/stereo/ascii_PLASTIC_10m_new.html, courtesy                        
#                               of C.T. Russell.  COHOWeb's magnetic field hourly averages were created at                            
#                               GSFC/SPDF by averaging over the six 10-min averages falling within each hour.                         
#                                Hourly plasma parameter data, including plasma flow direction angles for STEREO-A                    
#                               but not yet for STEREO B (as of 7/11/2010), were obtained from UNH via http://fiji.sr.unh.edu/1dmax_as
#     NSSDC_ID                 2006-047A

#     LOGICAL_SOURCE           stb_coho1hr_merged_mag_plasma
#     LOGICAL_SOURCE_DESCR     Merged hourly magnetic field, plasma and ephermis data
#     PI_NAME                  Natasha Papitashvili
#     PI_AFFILIATION           NASA/GSFC
#     MISSION_GROUP            STEREO

# 12. SW plasma density
